                     <div data-reactid="442">
                      <div data-reactid="443">
                       over-sized, spacious 1 bedroom on ground floor of Spanish Revival home in a quiet residential area of Hollywood, walk to everything Hollywood. Excellent base for your stay in LA, conveniently located for walking metro and buses. Large kitchen, free off street parking, reliable wifi. Loving details, arty and comfortable.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="444">
                       Walk everywhere in Hollywood! Coveted free parking space right in front of the home for your car. Super spacious 1 Bedroom /1 Bath Spanish style home, full of light, with high coved ceilings and 1921 Batchelder fireplace The living room is 20 by 32 ft, the bedroom is 16/18 ft . Large L- shaped eat-in kitchen with washer. Hardwood floors throughout, tile bath. Ceiling to floor windows in the living room. Bathroom is off the bedroom, wireless internet is extremely reliable throughout. Air conditioning, so the apartment is comfortable in all weather. In addition to comfy queen bed, there's a full size futon in the living room. (and queen-size air bed if needed), Fast wireless internet throughout; DirecTV cable and HBO channels. Small patio and flowers, property has a lime tree, climbing roses and a back garden shared by neighbors. This is an amazing neighborhood -- the historic Hollywood district, full of lore, yet this is a completely residential street with friendly, longtime neighbors. This is one of the oldest neighborhoods in Hollywood. A lot of the houses are Spanish revival, Craftsman bungalows and the usual Los Angeles mix. Off street parking in driveway right in front of the apartment. Very safe and quiet and only a 6 minute walk to center of Hollywood. Equidistant between 2metro stations: Hollywood and Vine and Hollywood and Highland. Buses 1 block from apt, on Santa Monica Blvd, transfers to beach area and elsewhere. This is a very central neighborhood in LA, equidistant to everything else. short walk to: Hollywood and Vine, the Capitol building, Avalon, the Hollywood and Highland complex, Gruaman's Chinese theatre, Arclight cinema, grocery stores,numerous cafes and restaurants, Hollywood Walk of Fame, Roosevelt Hotel and largest Southern Cal. Farmer's Market on Sunday mornings at Ivar and Cahuenga. The apartment is one block from the Theatre District. We also have Golden Bridge Yoga on Highland and De Longpre, Life Food Organic, TenderGreens, Stella for Italian food, Mozza for great pizza, Chipotle Grill, Juicy Burger, Cafe de Solar (great internet cafe), and tons of other great eateries. Comfy, roomy internet cafe 1 block away in Santa Monica Blvd: Hudson Cafe and the theatre district The location is perfect for visiting the Hollywood area, Universal Studios - 3 miles north, is accessible with a five minute metro ride-- and also central to visit other LA communities including Larchmont, WeHo, The Farmer's market at Third and Fairfax, the Grove, Los Feliz, Downtown, The North East side (NELA), the Valley, Griffith Park, Runyon Canyon and the beach. The apartment can accommodate up to 4 people. All bed linens and towels provided. FYI: LA city charges 14% 'transient residence' tax on any stay less than 30 days. Please also note: the piano is no longer here. Place is far larger than it looks in the pics.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="445">
                       I love this neighborhood, and many who know of it or find out about it agree that it's a find. It's a great residential neighborhood with long time tenants and owners who love it so much that it becomes home for good. It's very safe, diverse, and very close to things. You get the feeling you are in the center of things here. I would prefer to live in this neighborhood than any other in LA because of my neighbors and the vibe on this block! You are very close to all the new happenings near Sunset /Vine/Hollywood Blvd and all the new development.

                       PRIVATE APARTMENT: Unlike many other guest rentals you will find this upper flat is used exclusively to host guests, that means it is 100% private and 100% yours for the duration of your visit. Come enjoy our top floor flat in a renovated 1920's two story building professionally designed by Jennifer Ridel of Studio Fenix|LA and located in the trendy Melrose - Fairfax district! Close to West Hollywood, Hollywood, Beverly Hills, Miracle Mile and Hancock Park, you will feel right at home everything you need for a short or long term stay. This well laid out flat is on the upper level of a 5 unit building and shares no common walls with any neighbors. There is both a front and rear secure entry to the building with easy access via lockbox. On-Site Parking Included! BEDROOM Relax in the comfort of a QUEEN size bed with four pillows and luxury linens that will help you catch up on your sleep. Lounge in our double setee while you catch up on some reading. Hang your clothes in our large, walk in closet, complete with full size ironing board and iron. Draw the black out shades at days end close yourself in for the night. BATHROOM Double set of towels, soap, professional blow dryer, Cottonelle toilet paper (not the cheap stuff!) KITCHEN Adequately appointed kitchen complete with double sink, full size fridge and freezer, full size range oven, microwave, toaster, coffee press and kettle and service for four. High Speed WiFi internet lets you connect all of your WiFi enabled devices. OFFICE Separate your work and play with our cozy window office. LOCATION The immediate neighborhood has plenty of shops and restaurants, both fine and casual and backed by quite residential homes. Satiate your inner foodie with a visit to the highly acclaimed Mozza, relax with coffee and the papers across the street at Stir Crazy, stand on line at the world famous Pink's Hotdogs, grab some vegan delights at M Cafe de Chaya. The location is an ideal spot if you are looking to check out Los Angeles like a local. You are in close proximity to The Grove and The Farmers Market (at the Grove), Hollywood and Highland where you can catch the Red Line to Universal Studios, The Beverly Center and Larchmont Village. Locals in the area hang out on Melrose, La Brea, 3rd, Beverly, Larchmont Blvd and Highland Ave. LA is a driving city, so most visitors rent a car however if you find yourself without you will find yourself walking distance to all that you need for a great experience and just a block away from major North - South and East - West bus routes. We look forward to your inquiry and are here to answer any questions that you may have.

                       This private, gated guesthouse with secure off-street parking and a garden deck is in the heart of Hollywood, steps from the Walk of Fame, on a residential street. Amenities include air conditioning, heating, a full kitchen, WiFi and DirectTV.

                      <div data-reactid="1525">
                       Location. Location. Location. This private guesthouse completely renovated in October of 2013 has all the amenities you expect. Air conditioning. Heating. Wireless internet. A full kitchen. Direct TV on a 32 inch high definition television. A large ceiling fan. Gated parking. There is also a garden deck for you to enjoy. This is strictly a vacation rental property - the owner lives in the main house on the same property. The guesthouse was professionally decorated and is professionally cleaned. You will not be living in the midst of someone else's stuff - this property is maintained with the diligence and care of a professional hotel, but with the comfort and convenience of living in your own guesthouse. Did we mention location? The house is in central Hollywood, on a gated property. The sites and sounds of Hollywood are all in walking distance. You are in the heart of it all, mere blocks away from the Hollywood commercial district, the Hollywood Bowl, the Hollywood Walk of Fame, the Jimmy Kimmel Show, and all the nightlife and site seeing options that make Hollywood famous, on a residential street that is quiet by city standards. Need to drive? The 101 is a five minute drive away and there is gated parking. And, you can walk to the Red Line if you prefer taking LA's subway system. Downtown, Universal Studios and the Valley, West Hollywood and Beverly Hills are all easily accessible. And, a Hollywood Dash stop is literally outside the home's front gate. The guesthouse sleeps two, with a main room, a kitchen, a bath room, and the garden deck.

                       Luxury 1 BR in remodeled Spanish Building on quiet street just blocks away from downtown Hollywood.

                      <div data-reactid="1652">
                       SCENE MEETS ZEN. Perfect for single or couple that wants to walk to all things Hollywood but escape to a beautiful getaway apartment. This is a stunning little retreat that looks and lives like a vacation resort. It’s bright, airy, immaculate and incredibly private, with a huge window looking out onto a private outdoor garden space. AMENITIES. This unit really is one-of-a-kind — bright, airy, immaculate and incredibly private. Designed by an architect, this space was created by someone who planned to live there. It has polished concrete floors and windows on three sides; a clean kitchen with new cabinets, new stainless steel appliances and a separate pantry; an oversized shower with glass tile and a sun window; wifi; flat-screen TV and more. PRIVACY. My favorite feature is a mature outdoor garden surrounded by a 12’ tall privacy hedge. Step into the sunshine and fresh air; enjoy hummingbirds and butterflies with your morning coffee and croissant. For real. This place will make you feel like you’re staying at a trendy resort for a fraction of the price. It’s most often described as sexy, amazing and incredibly comfortable. If that’s how you like to live, you can count on having a great vacation experience in L.A. with us. LOCATION: Centrally located in hip and happening Hollywood, it’s just a few minutes’ walk to the Hollywood Walk of Fame, W Hotel complex, Capital Records, Pantages Theater, Hollywood Forever movies, Cinerama Dome and Arclight, countless bars, clubs, restaurants, nightlife, shopping, market, boutiques and more. Close to studios, metro station and bus lines. Spend a Sunday morning strolling through the local farmer’s market and then hit Amoeba to find that recording you can’t find anywhere. It’s a five-minute drive to Universal Studios or Griffith Park, just a little farther to hipsterland in Silverlake. It’s just down the street from a banana bungalow on Hlwd Blvd, so you know it’s a convenient location for visitors. PERFECTION. This apartment is beautifully furnished with an impeccable eye — it’s good to have friends who are architects and designers. If your environment matters to you, you’ll love my place! minimal
